schemas/constructs/v1beta2/design/api.yml	Schema "MesheryPatternPage" mixes JSON-tag casing conventions across its properties — camel: [resultType]; lowercase: [page, patterns]; snake: [page_size, total_count]. Partial casing migrations are forbidden under the canonical identifier-naming contract. If the wire format must change, introduce a new API version and migrate every property consistently. See AGENTS.md § "Casing rules at a glance" and docs/identifier-naming-migration.md §9.

schemas/constructs/v1beta2/relationship/api.yml	Schema "RelationshipDefinition" mixes JSON-tag casing conventions across its properties — camel: [evaluationQuery, schemaVersion, subType]; lowercase: [capabilities, id, kind, metadata, model, selectors, status, type, version]; snake: [model_id]. Partial casing migrations are forbidden under the canonical identifier-naming contract. If the wire format must change, introduce a new API version and migrate every property consistently. See AGENTS.md § "Casing rules at a glance" and docs/identifier-naming-migration.md §9.
